<Time>1575981282955< /Time><review>I've come back here numerous times and I've got to say that I think my rating has been too low.  The fact that they make a wonderful vegan noodle soup and you can modify it anyway you want is such a nice thing.  They also have done away with the free cream cheese dumpling and now serves you edamame for free is a much better option for me.  I love putting them in my soup to get more veggies.  I also love their eggplant you can add to your ramen.  It is so tender and tasty with the broth they serve it in.  Still don't really like the boiled cabbage with carrots as it's  pretty boring for $2.50 but last I asked they will bring you broccoli as a side.  I usually get the tofu as that is plentiful and really tasty with the soup.  As far as the noodles goes I love the Soba and pay the extra $.50 cents to get that versus the ramen noodles but both are excellent.  Lastly the service here is quite good and very friendly.  They are constantly refilling my glass with ice water.  Most places now only serve room temp water from a tap and I always hate that.  This is clean tasting water that is ice cold.  Would love for them to add a few more veggie dishes like maybe Yakisoba or a another tofu dish. But for now I'm ok just ordering my regular bowl of noodles and adding whatever I am in the mood for.  Oh and for Los Altos norms the prices are not all that bad either.  Glad to up my rating to reflect my most recent experiences.  Good Going Charley!<//review>< rate>

<Time>1560735354551< /Time><rating>3< /rating>< text>
I have a few things to share about the place and the service, less about the food. The most important one - THE TIP IS INCLUDED IN THE BILL!

The good
* The freshly squeezed juices are soooo good! Very refreshing, although not cheap (~$6-7 for a medium sized glass)
* The food is fresh and good - Chocolate chip pancakes were delicious!

The bad
* PSA! The tip is already included when you get the check! - They never mentioned that, and I found out about it a few hours too late. I know it's my fault as you should scan the bill and verify, but that usually happens when there is a big party - We were four people, and no one mentioned anything about it. Really annoying and makes you feel cheated.
* The place is tiny but we were ready for that and joined the queue from home via Yelp. When we came, we were the third party in line (total of four people). With all that, we've waited over 50 minutes to be seated. Not sure if we got unlucky, but this something you need to take into consideration
* Brunch - The potatoes were good, a bit too salty, the eggs were great, but no salt or pepper at all.  Kind of weird.

Due to the issue with the tip, while the place is nice, I feel like it is not entirely honest and I won't be coming back.<//text>

< Review>
Wait: As there are very few brunch spots around the Inner Richmond, this place tends to have a 20-30 min wait. They do have the Yelp reservation system though, so you can reserve your spot in line ahead of time without having to actually wait outside.

Ambiance: The place is pretty small, but has a cozy feel. Even though it's usually busy, service is pretty fast and staff is friendly and attentive.

Food: I had the Crazy Moco with a side of bacon. The pork katsu was slightly dry, but the crust was super crispy. The gravy was very rich and had a nice little kick (though I could use a little more). The bacon was nice and thick, but still crispy. My companion had the crab Benedict. The eggs were poached well and the hollandaise was nice and creamy. The crab wasn't too sweet, but was still good.

Price: The portions are quite big here, but the price seemed a bit too high for what you are getting. The Benedict dish ended up being around $30.< /Review>

I used this service on a recent trip to San Jose, flying into and out of San Francisco airport. Both drivers I had were fantastic; very professional, accommodating, thoughtful and punctual.
I appreciated that for my very early morning pick up Ron was considerate of it being so early and not trying to make lots of small talk (not that I mean to sound rude, but as I am not a morning person, not having to chat continually was nice.). Also during the drive for my pick up from the airport on the way to San Jose, the driver (I am so sorry I can't remember his name.) had lots of interesting tidbits about California and the area I was staying that were a nice set up for my vacation.
Lastly, I was very impressed with the communication through their website! My questions were answered right away and setting up my pickups was a breeze.

I was nervous about using a service I knew nothing about, but after reading all the good reviews and now my own experience I would use Emerald Limousine again in a heart beat.  Their rates were good, the drivers very punctual and capable, cars were extremely clean and the service outstanding. I felt safe and confident in their capable hands.

< Review>
In California just this past weekend 04_12_19, we used the service to go from SFO airport to Santa Rosa, CA round trip over a weekend.  The Drivers were on time and we were delivered on time but that's the extent of the positive feedback.  Besides being very expensive (I know it's California) but the Vehicles were in serious disrepair!  It appears that 5 Emeralds is a driver brokerage service as one of the drivers was monitoring Multiple Services throughout our trip.  The First Car was a Lincoln Aviator and it was torn up on the inside and had a Huge Crack all the way across the windshield, Seats and consoles were torn and just really beat up.  The car shook significantly each time he applied the brakes, the Driver was eating Chips our of the passenger seat the entire 1.5 hr trip (really) we were just thankful to get where we were going SAFELY.  We considered multiple times about cancelling our return trip and finding another service but we thought that was a "fluke" surely the next one would be better on the return.  We were pleasantly surprised when we got picked up for the return trip it was a very clean and nice Lincoln Navigator and it was clean and neat on the inside, BUT...  about 30 minutes into our trip back the Transmission started slipping and shaking!  Really? There were several hills where the driver had to let way off the gas just to get the transmission to catch and Cars were flying Up the hill past us as we putted up at 28 mph hoping to get to the top.  I started my UBER app just to see who was in the area.  Again very stressful.  We finally made it back to the airport but I'm Glad we padded our time by 2 additional hours so we weren't late...  I Don't recommend 5 Emeralds.<//Review>

Last two trips weren't great experiences.

On the most recent trip, I explained in the booking request that our kids are 2 & 4, and our reservation confirmation correctly stated "two forward facing toddler seats". But the vehicle arrived with 2 unharnessed booster seats only, labelled 3-10 years. Instead of apologizing, the driver argued with us at the airport curbside that these seats were fine.

3 stars (rather than 2 or 1) because we've had previous trips with five emerald that ran smoothly.  However after 2 bad trips in a row we will be going elsewhere for our next trip.<//review>

< review>
Purchased a truck from Redding Car and Truck two months ago. I asked to see the pre-sale inspection report and the sales person stated, "We don't do that." They did provide me with a list of repairs they had made and guaranteed me, "We wouldn't sell it if it had issues. Our name is on the line." That being said, they have a list of repairs they still need to make and I have not heard a word from them.
Brake issues, door panel and dash are broken, washer fluid reservoir is broken, heater doesn't work, gas guage doesn't work, electrical issues and the list goes on.
I have text messages from the salesperson apologizing for selling me such a mess of a vehicle. I've called Mike to see what is going on with the repairs and he said he would order parts. Never heard from him again. No date as to when the parts will arrive or when the truck will be repaired.
Poor customer service.
If you're wondering about all the 5-star reviews, they ask you to post a 5-star so they can get their bonus.< /review>
